## Diagram 2

```mermaid
graph TD
    PC[PackageContainer]
    PCE[PackageContainerEvent]
    PCTTL[PackageContainerToTripLeg]
    TL[TripLeg]
    PCEX[PackageContainerException]
    PCET[PackageContainerExceptionType]
    DLOC[LocationNode dloc]
    ELOC[LocationNode eloc]
    
    PC -->|parent_child| PCE
    PC -->|parent_child| PCTTL
    PC -->|parent_child| PCEX
    PC -->|peer code_org| DLOC
    PCTTL -->|peer trip_leg_id| TL
    PCEX -->|peer exception_type_id| PCET
    PCE -->|peer code_org| ELOC
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start([Start: PartviewGraphReduceTask])
    Start --> Init[Initialize Databricks Session]
    Init --> Storage[Create StorageClient]
    Storage --> CreateNodes[Create All Nodes:<br/>PackageContainer, Events,<br/>Exceptions, TripLegs, Locations]
    CreateNodes --> CreateGraph[Create GraphReduce<br/>with PackageContainer as parent]
    CreateGraph --> AddNodes[Add all nodes to graph]
    AddNodes --> AddEdges[Add entity edges:<br/>parent-child & peer relationships]
    AddEdges --> Plot[Plot graph to HTML]
    Plot --> Transform[Execute do_transformations]
    Transform --> AddTS[Add transformTs column]
    AddTS --> Write[Write to Delta table]
    Write --> Output[Write completion marker]
    Output --> End([End])
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Luigi
    participant Task as PartviewGraphReduceTask
    participant Spark as DatabricksSession
    participant GR as GraphReduce
    participant Storage as StorageClient
    participant Delta as Delta Table
    
    Luigi->>Task: run()
    Task->>Spark: Create session
    Spark-->>Task: Session created
    Task->>Storage: Initialize StorageClient
    Task->>Task: Instantiate all nodes
    Task->>GR: Create GraphReduce
    Task->>GR: add_node() x7
    Task->>GR: add_entity_edge() x7
    GR->>GR: plot_graph()
    GR->>GR: do_transformations()
    GR-->>Task: Transformed DataFrame
    Task->>Task: Add transformTs column
    Task->>Delta: Write DataFrame
    Delta-->>Task: Write complete
    Task->>Task: Write completion marker
    Task-->>Luigi: Task complete
```

    }

    }
